</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AstroNova Reports Fiscal 2025 First Quarter Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Company Reiterates Fiscal 2025 Full-Year Outlook</I> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="14%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Earnings conference call at 9:00 a.m. ET today </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>West Warwick, R.I., June</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;6, 2024</B> &#150; AstroNova, Inc. (Nasdaq: ALOT), a global leader in data visualization technologies, today
announced financial results for its fiscal 2025 first quarter ended April&nbsp;27, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CEO Commentary </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our first-quarter results were hampered by supplier shortages and an order <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">push-out</FONT> by one customer, both of
which we expect to be remedied this fiscal year,&#148; said Greg Woods, President and Chief Executive Officer of AstroNova. &#147;In our Test and Measurement segment, shipments of certain legacy aerospace printers were delayed due to the inability
of suppliers to provide components on time. We are working closely with those suppliers and expect to have the shortages resolved in the third quarter of this year. Longer-term, we are on track with our plans to replace the majority of our legacy
aerospace printers with our newer, more advanced ToughWriter-branded printers. Today, ToughWriter printers account for approximately 36% of our total aerospace printer shipments. Completing the transition will result in a more efficient supply
chain, lower manufacturing costs and a streamlined parts and services experience for our OEM and airline customers. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In our Product Identification
segment, the year-over-year decrease in first-quarter revenue was partly the result of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">push-out</FONT> of a $4.5&nbsp;million order for next-generation mail-handling equipment introduced last fall at the PRINTING
United Expo,&#148; Woods said. &#147;We are in the process of adding a customer-requested design enhancement; we expect to complete that enhancement and begin volume shipments on that order in the second quarter of this year. Despite the lower top
line, the Product Identification segment&#146;s operating profit margin increased 290 basis points during the quarter. This result reflected efficiencies gained from our strategic realignment of the segment in
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2023,</FONT> which included the exit from certain older, lower-margin or low-volume products.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Outlook </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Looking ahead, we are excited about the prospects for both segments of our business,&#148; Woods said. &#147;With our recent acquisition of
Portugal-based MTEX NS, we have significantly strengthened our position in the color digital printing market. In addition to expanding our color labeling business, we now have a much larger footprint in both the durable and flexible packaging market
segments. This greatly expanded range of AstroNova products was showcased over the past 10 days in Germany at drupa 2024, the world&#146;s preeminent printing trade fair. Our sales team met with a record number of current and prospective customers,
and many have already placed orders. Within our T&amp;M segment, we continue to win key defense programs for our data acquisition recorders and gain traction with the ToughWriter transition. We are on track to meet our fiscal full-year 2025
expectations for organic revenue growth in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits and Adjusted EBITDA margins of 13% to 14%.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Q1 FY 2025 Financial Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Segment Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product Identification </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Product Identification (PI) segment revenue was $23.2&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with $25.1&nbsp;million in the same period of
fiscal 2024. Segment operating profit was $3.0&nbsp;million, or 12.9% of segment revenue, compared with segment operating profit of $2.5&nbsp;million, or 10.0% of segment revenue, in the first quarter of fiscal 2024, reflecting a more favorable mix
in the 2025 period. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Test&nbsp;&amp; Measurement (T&amp;M) segment revenue was $9.8&nbsp;million in the first quarter of fiscal 2025, compared with $10.3&nbsp;million in the first
quarter of fiscal 2024, primarily as a result of lower hardware revenue. Segment operating profit was $1.7&nbsp;million, or 17.6% of segment revenue, compared with segment operating profit of $2.1&nbsp;million, or 20.1% of segment revenue, in the
first quarter of fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Earnings Conference Call Information </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova will discuss its fiscal 2025 first quarter financial results in an investor conference call at 9:00 a.m. ET today. To access the conference call,
please dial (833) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">470-1428</FONT> (U.S. and Canada) or (404) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">975-4839</FONT> (International) approximately 10 minutes prior to the start time and enter access code 832846. A real-time
and an archived audio webcast of the call will be available through the &#147;Investors&#148; section of the AstroNova website, <U>https://investors.astronovainc.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to financial measures prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP), this news release contains the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure Adjusted EBITDA, which we define as earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and amortization, stock-based compensation and acquisition-related costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova believes that the inclusion of this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure helps investors gain a meaningful
understanding of changes in the Company&#146;s core operating results and can help investors who wish to make comparisons between AstroNova and other companies on both a GAAP and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis.
AstroNova&#146;s management uses this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure, in addition to GAAP financial measures, as the basis for measuring its core operating performance and comparing such performance to that of
prior periods and to the performance of its competitors. This measure is also used by the Company&#146;s management to assist with their financial and operating decision-making. Please refer to the financial reconciliation table included in this
news release for a reconciliation of this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure to the most directly comparable GAAP measure for the three months ended April&nbsp;27, 2024 and April 29, 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About AstroNova </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AstroNova (Nasdaq: ALOT), a global
leader in data visualization technologies since 1969, designs, manufactures, distributes, and services a broad range of products that acquire, store, analyze, and present data in multiple formats. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Product Identification segment provides a wide array of digital,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-to-end</FONT></FONT> product marking and identification solutions, including hardware, software, and supplies for OEMs, commercial printers, and brand owners. The Test and
Measurement segment provides products designed for airborne printing solutions, avionics, and data acquisition. Our aerospace products include flight deck printing solutions, networking hardware, and specialized aerospace-grade supplies. Our data
acquisition systems are used in research and development, flight testing, missile and rocket telemetry production monitoring, power, and maintenance applications. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>
